	<script>
		var redirectionCountDown = {
			code: "",
			url: "",
			isActive: false,

			start: function(time, code, url){
				this.code = code;
				this.url = url;
				this.isActive = true;
				this.displayTime(time);
			},

			stop: function(){
				this.isActive = false;
			},

			displayTime: function (time) {
				if(redirectionCountDown.isActive){
					if (time >= 0) {
						document.getElementById('redirect-countdown').textContent = 'Redirection to the site in '+ redirectionCountDown.code +' in ' + time + 's';
						setTimeout(redirectionCountDown.displayTime, 1000, time - 1);
					}else{
						chooseAndRedirect(redirectionCountDown.code, redirectionCountDown.url);
					}
				}else{
					document.getElementById('redirect-countdown').textContent = '';
				}
			}
		};

		function chooseAndRedirect(code, url){
			redirectionCountDown.stop();
			chooseLang(code);
			location.href=url;
		}
		function chooseLang(code) {
			setCookie("chooselang",code,365);
		}
	</script>
	</body>
</html>
